[00:36:16]           exit \$RET" \
[00:36:16]         INT TERM ERR
[00:36:16] 
[00:36:16]     # Start saving everything into our history
[00:36:16]     trap save_history DEBUG
[00:36:16] else
[00:36:16]     # If we're running in `sh` or something like that, we need a
[00:36:16]     # slightly slimmer set of traps. :(
[00:36:16]     trap "RET=\$?; \
[00:36:16]           echo Previous command exited with \$RET >&2; \
[00:36:16]           set +e +x; \
[00:36:16]           save_env; \
[00:36:16]           exit \$RET" \
[00:36:16]         EXIT INT TERM
